Current Affairs Commentary

The Yellow River Flood Disaster 26

For half a month, the Yellow River flood disaster has become increasingly serious. At the end of July, the waters in various parts of Shaanxi province rose simultaneously due to subterranean surges. The Jing and Wei Rivers destroyed their channels, and there were also reports of flash floods in the upper reaches of the Yellow River. Although a disaster occurred in Shaanxi, the scope was not very large. However, at the beginning of August, the water levels in the upper, middle, and lower reaches of the Yellow River increased. At that time, in Changyuan, Hebei province, because troops were suppressing bandits, the bandits secretly destroyed two sections of the river embankment, flooding the rural villages, creating a quite tragic disaster. Extending to Shandong province, the area of terror gradually widened. Recently, in counties such as Xixi and Ciwen in western Henan, the Yellow River waters have overflowed their channels, and the Rongze River has overflowed its banks, reaching Zhengzhou. The floodwaters are heading east, threatening Kaifeng and tending to enter the silted Yellow River. Lanfeng has already been affected. To the north, Lisheng Village in Shandong, and to the east, the northwestern counties of Jiangsu, all face an untenable situation. The threat of the flood disaster has now reached four or five provinces. It is not just a report of disaster in the Central Plains.

Those who discuss the water conservancy of the Yellow River say that since the thirteenth year of the Guangxu reign of the previous Qing Dynasty (1887), the river channel has been stable for more than forty years, and there has been no news of flooding, showing a trend toward becoming more standardized. The Yellow River's surface is higher than the flatlands on both sides, and the severity of its floods is well-known both domestically and abroad. Even within the 267 years of the Qing Dynasty, there were 39 breaches. Before the thirteenth year of Guangxu, there was a flood disaster on average every six years. The reason why there has been no news of flooding in the nearly forty years since then, according to water conservancy experts, is due to the Yangwu Dike and the bridge protection dams of the Pinghan Railway, which have gradually guided the river into a proper course, and the stone protecting the cliffs along the banks, which has gradually strengthened the riverbanks. However, the biggest reason is that in the tributaries and river basins of western Henan, more and more people are diverting river water for irrigation, with crisscrossing channels, enough to reduce the flow of the Yellow River. The wasteland in the upper reaches has been cultivated year by year, so that most of the rainwater does not enter the Yellow River but is absorbed by the newly cultivated land first. However, this diversion of water for irrigation and the absorption of water by cultivated land were not done intentionally for water conservancy purposes. Therefore, they cannot fundamentally eliminate the water damage of the Yellow River. Moreover, from Rongze eastward, the degree to which the riverbed is higher than the flat ground gradually increases. Near Lanfeng, the land gradually becomes higher than the river. But within this large segment, we have not heard of any water conservancy projects that would have been of any benefit. However, considering the indirect ability of opening channels and cultivating wasteland in western Henan and the upper reaches to reduce the damage from the Yellow River floods, amidst this terror of the flood disaster, we cannot help but hope that the officials of the provinces in the Yellow River basin will, on the one hand, strive to encourage the development of this undertaking to increase its effectiveness in preventing disasters, and, on the other hand, supervise and encourage local people in those counties where this undertaking has not yet been carried out to rise up and start it. In this way, the number of channels will increase day by day, the power of the Yellow River can be reduced, and the ground that absorbs water will gradually increase, so that the river water can be prevented from bursting its banks and causing harm.

In the midst of the previous terror of the Yangtze River flood disaster, we exhausted our voices in appealing on behalf of the people of the provinces along the river. Fortunately, the river water gradually receded, and a major disaster was avoided. In recent days, the central water conservancy agencies and the authorities of various provinces have gathered to discuss disaster prevention and relief, and to carry out emergency work. The old events are repeating themselves, and they are extremely busy. It seems unnecessary for us to repeat the old articles. We only hope that after fortunately avoiding a major disaster, we will engage in fundamental water conservancy projects.

The End of the Era of Terror in Cuba

Dr. Cespedes Elected Provisional President 27

Martial Law Declared in the Capital, All Efforts to Restore Order

Machado Flees to the Bahamas

The era of terror in Havana, Cuba has come to an end. The new leader, Cespedes, having been recommended by Congress, will take office as provisional president tonight. His first act after taking office will be to declare martial law so that the military can take appropriate measures to restore order. Next, he will call on the people to be calm, abide by the law, and return to work. Cespedes comes from a prominent family and is unanimously supported by the Liberal Party (i.e., the ruling party that supported the old President Machado) and various revolutionary parties, and has received the informal endorsement of the U.S. government. According to news from the provinces, he is also supported by the rural areas. At a time when the whole country is looking forward to governance, it is expected that he will be able to reform and innovate, wash away the violent rule, and revive the people's livelihood. (National Telegram, 12th)

Today, the Cuban fortress in Havana fired a 21-gun salute, indicating that the Cuban army supports the election of Dr. Cespedes, the Minister of Education, as provisional president to succeed Machado. All political parties have also expressed their agreement. The authorities are now working hard to restore security and order in the capital. Machado's property is now heavily guarded. This morning, the General Staff ordered the army to occupy Havana and send troops to patrol the streets, stopping any actions that disturb public order. Machado has fled by plane to Nassau, Bahamas. (Reuters, 12th)

Voluntary Peaceful Provisional President's Proclamation to the People 28

Havana Dr. Cespedes officially assumed the position of acting president last night and issued a proclamation to the people, which stated, [I

follow the aspirations of all who hope for justice, peace, and patriotism to assume the head of state. I have taken office as president because the country is in danger, and my duty is to save the country in an effective way.] (Havas, 12th)

Abandoned by All, the Former President Leaves the Capital by Plane 29

Havana Former President Machado, hearing that popular resentment was boiling and that more than a thousand rioters were about to attack the presidential palace, signed his final order and left the capital by plane to avoid popular anger. Former Secretary of State Ferrara also sneaked out when the mob arrived at his home, fleeing to Miami, USA, by plane. When the plane departed, it was strafed by machine guns fired by the military, but fortunately it was not hit. His home was destroyed by the mob.

Signing an Order to Appoint Herrera as Provisional Executive 30

Earlier this morning, Machado, having been informed that the public's mood was turbulent and difficult to control, and fearing that it would be unfavorable to him, was advised by military leader De Cedas to go to his villa outside the capital for temporary refuge. Machado agreed and signed an order appointing Herrera, the chief of the army and navy, as provisional executive, but stipulated that Herrera should appoint Cespedes as Secretary of State, because according to the Cuban constitution, when the president dies or leaves office, the Secretary of State automatically becomes provisional president. De Cedas then prepared an armored car and sent heavy troops to protect and carry Machado to his villa outside the city, and then hired a plane to leave the capital. It is said that the police chief and the mayor of Havana accompanied him. According to unconfirmed news, Machado's plane landed on an island in the Bahamas, where a house had been prepared in advance. Herrera, after Machado left the capital, immediately went to the U.S. embassy to attend a meeting of various factions, and they agreed to elect Cespedes as provisional president. Congress will meet tonight under heavy guard to pass a resolution accepting Machado's resignation and supporting Cespedes as the new head of state. (

National Telegram, 12th)

The Army Minister Assumed Presidential Authority for Two Hours 31

Havana Army Minister Herrera was only provisional president for two hours before resigning and ceding the position to Dr. Cespedes. The military does not want Herrera to be president, but still recognizes him as Minister of the Army. (Havas, 12th)

Barely Escaping with His Life, the Former Secretary of State Flees to the United States 32

Miami (USA) Cuban Secretary of State Ferrara arrived here by plane today, stating during the transfer that Ferrara has resigned, but before the new Secretary of State takes office, the staff of the State Department will continue to handle routine official business as usual. (Reuters, 12th) Miami Cuban Secretary of State Ferrara, after arriving here, stated that before he fled Havana, he was almost murdered by rioters. They had broken into his home and killed one of his servants. He took the opportunity to escape while the rioters were attacking the inner door and went to the airport outside the city to take a plane here. He will stay here for a few days to observe the changes. (National News Agency, 12th)

Revolutionary Party Leaders Participate in Cabinet Formation 33

Havana The situation here is rather strange. It is generally believed that former President Menocal, the leader of the revolutionary party who is likely to be elected president, is still in Miami, USA, with his advisors and has not returned to the country. However, considering that Menocal did not send representatives to participate in the negotiations previously mediated by U.S. Ambassador Welles, it seems that he is no longer at the center of the situation. Colonel Alvarez, who is currently leading the revolutionary army in the area between the provinces of Oriente and Santa Clara, has been invited to the capital to jointly select cabinet members. Alvarez has been fighting the Machado government's army for more than a year, and his troops are well-equipped. He is also the first to contribute to the revolution. At this time, those who have the right to speak on cabinet formation include the leaders of various revolutionary parties. The parties currently in the capital include the Nationalist Party, the Student Party, and the ABC Party. The ABC Party is a secret organization that specializes in dealing with Machado's secret police and implementing a reciprocal plan of terrorism. (National Telegram, 12th) Night of Terror

Murder, Robbery, and Destruction of the Presidential Palace 34

Havana Yesterday and this morning were unusually chaotic, with frequent incidents, resulting in a total of twenty-one deaths and more than two hundred injuries. The military and police were unable to maintain order. The private residences of Machado and his associates were destroyed by rioters after the owners fled. Utensils were thrown into the streets, and valuables and clothing were looted. Government offices and government-run newspapers were also destroyed. The rioters then went to the presidential palace. During the disturbance, at least five plainclothes police officers were killed. The naval and army soldiers stationed at the palace wanted to suppress the riots, but were unable to do so. The flowers and trees in the palace were completely destroyed. According to the opinions of the general public, the collapse of the Machado government is now being appropriately celebrated. There have been recent reports that Havana Mayor Dr. Izquierdo was killed, but this has not yet been confirmed. Colonel Jiménez, the chief of secret detectives, shot and wounded a demonstrator while the public was fervently celebrating Machado's abdication. Soldiers, seeing this and feeling indignant, shot and killed Jiménez. Transportation between the capital and the interior is now blocked. (

Reuters, 12th)

Havana Mobs broke into the presidential palace and looted its silverware, paintings, and valuable carpets, and the military did not stop them. Tonight, the public is celebrating the success of the revolution, and the whole city is in a frenzy, cheering the name of the new head of state everywhere. At the same time, they are searching for and killing the secret police of the old president's era. Twelve people, including the chief of the secret police, have been arrested and killed, and their corpses are abandoned on the streets for all to despise. All those who held key positions in the Machado government are hiding and dare not come out. Even Herrera is hiding and has not been able to participate in the handover of administrative power to Cespedes. As for where he is hiding, it is expected to be in the U.S. embassy. (National Telegram, 12th)

The Mystery of Wu Teng's Death 37

Rumors Say He Was Poisoned with Arsenic

Staff Officer Sakata Died Before Wu Teng

Regarding the death of Wu Teng Xinyi, the former commander of the Kwantung Army and army general, on July 27, there are still many rumors about the cause of his death. Although the Japanese side has denied assassination, the Japanese here also believe that his death was not due to a normal illness. It is rumored that General Wu Teng was attacked by assassins in a car, or that he was injured by a landmine, or that a bomb was thrown. According to what was conveyed by his confidential staff, these rumors are not true. In fact, on the train from Dalian back to Changchun, arsenic was hidden in Wu Teng's food. Wu Teng and his staff officer, Colonel Sakata, were poisoned at the same time after eating it. However, Staff Officer Sakata was poisoned too severely. When the train arrived in Changchun, he died at his home shortly after. Wu Teng's poisoning was less severe, and he was treated by a doctor for detoxification, which extended his life for a few more days. In the end, he also died. After the death of Staff Officer Sakata, the Kwantung Army kept it secret. Three days after General Wu Teng's death, they announced the wrongful death of Staff Officer Sakata. Also, in Wu Teng's will, he mentioned that disputes among his subordinates were detrimental to the future governance of Manchuria and instructed the army to find a way to resolve this dispute, which shows the complexity of Wu Teng's cause of death. (Hualian News Agency Communication)

The Japanese Ministry of Foreign Affairs Decides to First Establish Economic Diplomacy Towards China 38

Using Tianjin and Qingdao as Bases

Adjusting Trade Relations with North China

According to the Dongbao, the Japanese foreign affairs authorities originally insisted on a fundamental policy of resolving disputes between China and Japan based on direct negotiations between China and Japan, and quietly waiting for the time when direct negotiations would begin. Now, in view of the free activities of anti-Japanese elements in China, and in order to cope with Soong Tzu-wen's anti-Japanese actions after returning to China, they have decided not to adhere to the previous passive observation policy towards China, but to take a more active diplomatic approach towards China. After fully consulting with Ambassador to China Ariyoshi and the new Director of the Asian Affairs Bureau of the Ministry of Foreign Affairs, Kuwajima, they will study a concrete plan to first establish economic diplomacy towards North China, using Tianjin and Qingdao as bases for Japanese economic diplomacy and adjusting trade relations with North China. (World News Agency)

The Triumphant Return of the Air Fleet is Enthusiastically Welcomed in Rome 42

Twenty-Three Planes Land in Ostia

Italian Prime Minister Embraces Balbo

Guilan Leaves Paved Along the Triumphal Arch, Women Contend to Offer Flowers

The Italian King Receives the Pilots in the Palace and Extends His Condolences

▲National, Rome, 12th An Italian air minister, Balbo, and his Atlantic crossing flight team arrived safely in Ostia at 8:30 tonight amidst thunderous cheers. Fifteen minutes later, the first nine aircraft had landed safely in succession. Balbo decided to send each aircraft to the airstrip across from Rome at Lido di Roma due to the late hour. Approximately ten minutes later, Balbo landed, and Prime Minister Mussolini immediately stepped forward to greet and embrace him. The people chanted the Giovinezza in unison, and the flight team's aircraft arrived at their destination in succession at this time.

▲Reuters, Rome, 12th General Balbo led his flight team to Ostia at 6:38 this evening. General Balbo's black aircraft led the way, followed closely by the other twenty-two aircraft. When the flight team appeared in the sky, millions of people cheered loudly, resounding through the sky. The military band then played the Fascist Party music. Italian Prime Minister Mussolini rushed to the place where the aircraft were parked and embraced General Balbo. Onlookers shouted, [Long live Balbo!] [Long live Mussolini!] General Balbo's wife led her three children to the field. When she kissed her husband, she was overwhelmed with joy and tears. When each pilot landed, the crowd cheered again, and General Balbo introduced the team members to the Prime Minister one by one. The team members then boarded twenty-four cars and headed for Rome. Mussolini and Balbo rode in the same car in front, followed by a hundred Fascist Party members on motorcycles in front of the car and a team of mounted police behind the car. At the time of departure, the public was ecstatic and reached the extreme. The procession arrived at the Palazzo Colonna, where the team members were again warmly welcomed. General Balbo responded to the welcoming speech by saying, [We are merely the small soldiers of the great commander!] Twenty-two aircraft were unable to first circle Rome due to bad weather, and landed at Ostia.

▲National, Rome, 13th The triumphant return of General Balbo's flight team yesterday was welcomed by the country in a grand occasion, second only to the triumph of the great General Caesar in ancient times. Near 6 PM, the aircraft appeared on the horizon, densely approaching the coast. At that time, more than one hundred thousand welcomers who had waited all day cheered thunderously. The last batch of aircraft in the team landed on the water at 7:15. This round trip crossed the Atlantic twice, leaving the country for forty-two days and flying twelve thousand five hundred miles. General Balbo was the first to land on the right side of the Grand Tribune at 6:20. He left the aircraft, wore the Fascist black shirt, approached Prime Minister Mussolini, and saluted and paid tribute to Mussolini and the crowd. The crowd shouted Long Live Balbo. A bridge was specially built on the waterfront, covered with flowers, for Balbo to walk on to land, but Balbo declined to enjoy this extravagant honor and jumped ashore from the wing of his aircraft. His wife, holding two young daughters, was also present at the time. The two young daughters kept shouting [Daddy]. At this time, the band played the national music. Mussolini stepped forward and embraced and kissed Balbo, which was the most enthusiastic salute in Italy. Mussolini then met with the team members one by one. Then, thousands of cars followed the team members to Rome. General Balbo gave a short speech at the Palazzo Colonna, thanking the people of the country, but his words were drowned out by cheers.

Balbo Promoted to Air Force General 43

▲Havas News Agency, Rome, 13th This morning, the Italian air fleet led by General Balbo was warmly welcomed by all sectors of society, no different from a triumphant return. The Italian king received the flight team members in the palace. They entered through the Arch of Constantine. No one has received this honor since 1527. Italian Prime Minister Mussolini awarded Air Minister Balbo the title of Air Force General. From 8 AM this morning, Fascist Party troops were stationed at the palace. The Italian King spoke with each pilot in his uniform for half an hour, and then led them to stand on the balcony. The crowd cheered wildly. The pilots then lined up to Piazza Navona. The streets were covered with laurel leaves. The wives and mothers of all the pilots who had previously died in the line of duty went to the Bonas Temple to present flowers to General Balbo. In front of the ancient Roman Theater, young Fascist Party members raised iron spears and crossed them to form a passage. The pilots passed under it. Officials were waiting in front of the Triumphal Arch. Noblewomen and ladies competed to offer flowers to General Balbo. Salutes were fired everywhere, and the troops saluted with their guns. Each pilot gathered on the Palatine Hill. At 10:30, Italian Prime Minister Mussolini arrived, wearing the uniform of the Party Army. General Balbo introduced the pilots one by one and said, [The reward we hope for in serving you is to be able to be driven and serve you one day]. The Italian Prime Minister said that the pilots had brought glory to the country, the Italian revolution, and aviation. What you have accomplished in this flight will not be seen again in several years. The Italian Prime Minister then kissed General Balbo and announced the Italian King's edict awarding Balbo the title of Air Force General. He also pinned a gold eagle on Balbo's chest. After the Italian Prime Minister announced the promotion edicts of each pilot, they all saluted the national flag and dispersed.

Full-Mongolian Academic Adventure Record (4) 65

Compiled Translation of Fragments of News from Osaka Mainichi, Asahi, Tokyo Hochi, and Asahi Newspapers, Because the Asahi Newspaper Still Lacks a Systematic Report

㈠ Discovery of a "Four-Not-Alike" Before Leaving Japan

On the 25th, the Japanese Man-Mongolian Academic Survey Team boarded the Hong Kong-bound ship in Kobe. Before the ship set sail, the team leader, Dr. Tokunaga, and Secretary Ihara went to the coast of Linzaki Village, west of Akashi, for a stroll. Suddenly, they discovered a valuable fossil of deer footprints on the Akashi coast, which is what is called a "Four-Not-Alike" in ancient Chinese books. These footprints are about 20 meters from the coast, on shale in the sea. There are four continuous prints. Dr. Tokunaga will soon publish a paper on these footprints of the "Four-Not-Alike." It has been found that the area along the coast nearby has been called "Deer Xiang" since ancient times, and fossils such as the teeth and tusks of elephants have often been found. According to Dr. Tokunaga, this is the second time that deer footprints have been discovered in Japan. About 20 years ago, they were discovered once near Hanamaki Onsen in Oshu. However, this is the first time that four footprints have been found in one place. Recently, a horn fossil was also discovered in the same area, which further confirms that it is a "Four-Not-Alike."

㈡ Discovery of New Plants in Lushun

The Man-Mongolian Academic Survey Team arrived in Dalian on the 27th. On the 28th, team leader Dr. Tokunaga led the members to visit Lushun. They first went to 203 Highland and Mount Jiguanshan to inspect the battlefields, and then visited the Lushun Museum, the zoo, and the botanical garden. From an academic standpoint, they have obtained unexpected gains immediately after entering Manchuria. That is, on 203 Highland, they discovered new species of Ai Peng (Artemisia) class, wild grapes, and chrysanthemums, as well as variants of cypress and juniper, obtaining valuable data in the botanical world. These plants were entrusted to Associate Professor Kishida and Professor Mori to make new specimens. At 4:30 PM on the 29th, they left Dalian and went north. On the 30th, they arrived in Fengtian. In addition to visiting various local agencies, they saw 20 stone steles with ancient Khitan characters at the private residence of Tang (the rebellious) Yu Lin, the headquarters of the Independent Garrison. The steles were one foot thick and four feet long and wide. They were originally discovered by the French Minister near Linxi, and after negotiating with Zhang Xueliang, it cost 20,000 yuan in shipping costs to send them to Tang's private residence. At noon on the same day, they collected plants and went to Beiling. At 3:00 PM, they took a car to Changchun. At 9:00 AM on the 31st, the car arrived at Changke Station. On the same day, they held a ceremony to form a team and formed a guard unit. In addition to visiting various agencies, they prepared a plan for the first step of exploration. On the afternoon of the 3rd, they arrived in Jinzhou and collected various reference materials. The structural geologist Kihachi Ihara and Dr. Saburo Shimizu formed the advance team. On the morning of the 4th, they departed from Jinzhou for Beipiao, entering the first gate of Rehe Northeast. The weather was unusually hot that day, with the temperature rising to 36 degrees Celsius. The survey team stayed in four hotels in Beipiao. In the afternoon, they transported food, equipment, and other items to Chifeng and Chengde separately. The 5th was the first day of work for the scientific exploration team. At 9:00 AM, the team members wore uniforms and gathered in front of the Beipiao Railway Station. Dr. Tokunaga gave instructions, saying, "From today, we will begin the scientific survey of Rehe. Each member will use their professional knowledge and give full play to their respective responsibilities in order to achieve distant goals." The team members were divided into classes according to department, with each class assigned six or seven soldiers. Dr. Tokunaga, Shimizu, Ihara, and the heads of each department began to investigate the Beipiao coal mine. Botanists Nakai and Honda entered the nearby mountains for inspection. Zoologists Mori and Kishida, as well as anthropologist Yahata and geographer Tada, all departed for their scheduled locations in succession.

㈢ Harvest in the Wilderness of Beipiao

At 9:00 AM on the 5th, the botany team, Nakai and Honda, carried collection equipment and went to the Wujianfang area. The zoology team, Hayata and Mori, carried insect nets and went to the mountains behind the coal mine. Team leader Tokunaga, Dr. Shimizu, and Mr. Ito specialized in investigating the Beipiao coal mine. Each team had six or seven guards. The geology and botany teams went to the remote area of ​​Yue. The botany team passed Wujianfang along the Beipiao River, exploring the embankments, wetlands, and grasslands along the river, and climbed the extremely high slopes, entering the pine forests and visiting a tribe under the jurisdiction of Old Mongolian King Ente. At this time, they suddenly received a report that a whirlwind was about to rise. For a time, the mountains, rivers, and natural scenery showed a desolate scene. By the evening, each team returned to Beipiao one after another. On this day, the botany team collected about 70 species of wild grasses and trees, including plants that were not seen in mainland Japan. According to Dr. Nakai, the soil near Beipiao is very fertile, and if pine trees are cultivated, they will definitely flourish. The area is deforested due to indiscriminate logging by the villagers, and only four or five plants such as Mongolian willow remain. The zoology team collected about 60 species of insects on this day, including a golden beetle that specializes in eating the feces of cattle and horses on the roadside and lives in holes in the ground. Anthropologist Dr. Yahata excavated many stones and earthenware of the Neolithic Age in the eastern slope of the mountains, and discovered objects related to bronze in Beipiao, all of which are valuable historical materials. In short, on the first day of the exploration work, each team had considerable gains. It is planned to depart for Chaoyang on the 7th.

Yellow River Warning in Bianyuan 66

The Wen County Embankment Overflowed, Turning into a Swamp. The Overflowed Water in Fan County and Rongze Counties is More Than Ten Feet Deep. There is News that the Yellow River Bridge on the Pinghan Railway is About to be Washed Away.

Liu Zhi Has Sent a Large Number of Vehicles to Rescue. The Residents of Kaifeng are Greatly Frightened Upon Hearing the News and are Fleeing in Droves. Lanfeng Has Been Flooded into the Old Riverbed, Very Close to the City.

The Situation in Shaan County is the Worst Flood in Fifty Years. The Hebei Changyuan Breach is Open. The Lu River Affairs Bureau is Preparing to Defend and Block the Flood.

Kaifeng Special News: Bianyuan is very close to the Yellow River, only 18 li from Liuyuan Kou in the north and only 25 li from Heigang Kou in the northwest. The water surface is usually about eight feet higher than the ground in Kaifeng. Once a breach occurs, it is like pouring water into a hole, which is extremely dangerous. Therefore, local people are often uneasy in the autumn and summer seasons. This year, the water volume has increased, and warnings have been frequent. On the night of the 8th, the water level in Wen County rose by two meters and one inch, and the dikes along the 6th, 7th, and 8th Forts overflowed for about ten li, turning dozens of square li outside the city into a swamp. As of yesterday, the water had surrounded the city, and the people's houses and property were all washed away. The water flow in Shaan County was 5,374 cubic meters larger than the previous maximum flow, which is the worst flood in fifty years. In Fan County, the dikes overflowed due to the Yellow River, and the water was more than ten feet deep on the ground. Many farmers who were escaping by boat capsized and died. The Ku River in the western end of Rongze has always been an internal flow of the Yellow River, but now, due to the large amount of water in the Yellow River, it has become a reverse flow. The railway tracks on both the north and south banks of the Pinghan Railway Bridge are slightly lower than the bridge body and were submerged by water. Zhengzhou North Thirty is about to become a swamp. The two express trains on the Pinghan Railway have been suspended. For more than a hundred li between the railway bridge and Heigang, many river embankments were submerged and collapsed. The water surface on the south bank is two or three feet away from the levee surface in most places, and three or four inches in some places, which is extremely dangerous. In the evening, Liu Zhi sent ten automobiles and forty large vehicles to transport materials, and dispatched 500 security team members, together with the Public Security Bureau and road workers, to rush to rescue the situation. However, few people in the city knew about it. It was not until the Republic Daily Extra was issued at about 10:00 PM that all entertainment venues were emptied, and the entire city was extremely tense. The number of cars rushing out of the north gate gradually increased, and the telephone of the River Affairs Bureau was constantly ringing. At midnight, the Public Security Bureau notified the citizens to prepare for the worst and sealed the southwest city gate. As a result, the residents were panicked and fled to public places with high-rise buildings. Longting and Henan University were extremely crowded. The sound of cars and the noise of the citizens continued all night. It was recently reported that the water level in Heigang had dropped, but all the projects were damaged. All the dignitaries are inspecting the area and supervising more than 1,500 soldiers and workers to rush to build the area. The situation in Zhengzhou is still extremely urgent. There are reports that the Yellow River Railway Bridge is about to be washed away, and the water in Lanfeng has flooded into the old riverbed, only a hundred steps away from the county seat. (August 11th, 10:00)

Jinan Correspondence: The Yellow River in Changyuan, Hebei, has breached. The River Affairs Bureau is very concerned that if the water is poured into Shandong, the three counties of Hetao Fan County, Yanggu County, and Shou Zhang County in the upper reaches will suffer. In addition to the Director, Zhang Lianjia, personally going to the upper reaches of the Tao Cheng Bu area on the north bank to inspect, he also ordered Pu County on the western border of Shandong to investigate and report the water situation of the breach. Today, according to a telegram from Zhang Guo Zhong, the county magistrate of Pu County, there are two breaches in Jindi Shitou Zhuang and Da Suo Zhuang in Changyuan, one more than 60 zhang wide and one more than ten zhang wide. The river water is now flowing to Weinan Irrigation area in Hua County, Henan, and has not yet flowed to Pu County. The smaller of the two breaches has been plugged, and the larger one is also being repaired. The River Affairs Bureau, in order to prevent all eventualities, is afraid that once the breach water is poured into the border counties, it will suffer losses. It is now ordering the upstream general section to actively transport materials and transfer workers to the north bank in preparation for defense and blockage. It is reported that the breach water is flowing slowly and weakly, and one of the two breaches has been blocked, and the situation has eased. It is probably not enough to cause harm. The upper, middle, and lower reaches of the Yellow River have all reported rising water due to continuous rain in recent days. According to the water level report obtained by the River Affairs Bureau this morning, the upper reaches rose more than two inches, the middle reaches rose more than four inches, and the lower reaches rose more than one inch. At noon, the water level was level. The report from Zhang Guo Zhong, the county magistrate of Pu County, on the breach is as follows: [Previously received a telegram stating that Jindi in Changyuan County, Hebei Province, was dug open by bandits in two places. According to investigation, the breaches are in Shitou Zhuang and Da Suo Zhuang, one more than 60 zhang wide and the other more than ten zhang wide. The river water flows out to Weinan Irrigation area in Hua County, Henan Province. Fortunately, it has not flowed to Pu County. The current Yellow River water level is dropping, and the dikes are exposed. The one that was more than ten zhang wide has been completed, and the one that is more than 60 zhang wide is still being repaired. I respectfully report this] (11th)

Jiang's Order to Provincial and County Magistrates in Bandit Suppression: Their Survival is Tied to the City's 68

No Embellishment, Complacency, Evasion of Responsibility Allowed; Those Who Can Defend But Fail To Will Face the Ultimate Penalty

Nanchang Communication: Chairman Chiang recently sent a telegram ordering all county magistrates in the bandit suppression provinces and districts to strive for vigorous efforts and to be determined to live or die with the city. Those who can defend but fail to do so will be treated as being cowardly in the face of battle and will be sentenced to the ultimate penalty. The original text is as follows: [Now is the time when the military operations of bandit suppression are being intensified. Regarding the elimination of local hidden dangers, the reconstruction of the bandit areas, and the assistance to military actions, all require the improvement of political efficiency. The implementation of general politics starts and ends at the county level. Therefore, the responsibility of the county magistrate is the most significant. Recently, it has been found that although there are not many county magistrates who are greedy and derelict in their duties, most of them excel at embellishment and consider complacency to be a good strategy. They evade responsibility and create a false appearance. Those who are clean, self-disciplined, and genuinely committed to their duties are often rigid and stick to the letter of the law, only concerned with completing the formalities of government orders but not seeking actual results. As a result, human and financial resources are wasted. For example, blockhouses are often built near the county seat but not in the villages; militia are only trained to assemble mechanically but are not asked if they can perform patrols and searches, or other bandit suppression tasks. Such examples are too numerous to list. It must be understood that the higher-level government can only indicate the objectives and principles of a policy. The steps of implementation, the speed of progress, depend on whether the county magistrate can understand the local conditions and adapt to the circumstances, and use the policy appropriately. What is even more regrettable is that we are lamenting the decline of the national spirit and thinking of ways to encourage and revitalize it. As a county magistrate, one should have the determination to serve the country and go to death, and to consider it shameful to seek safety in the face of danger. Since the rise of bandit suppression military operations, soldiers at the front lines have been dying in battle. However, most county magistrates either flee at the first sign of alarm or run away as soon as the bandits arrive. Those who can live or die with the city are as rare as phoenixes. Righteousness has disappeared and integrity is lost. How can the people stand when facing such officials? This must be rectified to change the atmosphere. Since last year, I, the Chairman, have been responsible for supervising the suppression, and have announced that the principle of "70% politics and 30% military" should be widely understood. Now, in order to improve political efficiency, I make an agreement with the county magistrates: From now on, each of you must deeply regret your past mistakes, strive for vigorous efforts, and completely abandon the bad habits of embellishment, complacency, superficial compliance, and secret resistance. All the things that should be done or reformed should be promoted practically, quickly, and resolutely, in the most economical and effective way. If a county is attacked by bandits and has sufficient regular self-defense forces, the magistrate must be responsible for defending to the death, awaiting the arrival of reinforcements. Otherwise, it will be treated as being cowardly in the face of battle and will be sentenced to the ultimate penalty. The district administrative commissioners are responsible for supervision. The quality of county administration and the bravery of the magistrates are their joint responsibility. The provincial government should provide proper guidance and strict supervision, and enforce the law without leniency. If the commanders-in-chief of each route and the general commanders have the authority to handle local party and government affairs, they are expected to be genuinely responsible within their respective jurisdictions and to supervise and encourage them strictly.] (August 10th)

The remaining guerrilla detachments and independent regiments have fewer than several hundred guns in total. More than 1,500 guns have been successively seized by the troops of Liang Guanying and others. The remaining forces are actually very few. Temporary houses will also be built in the important villages to provide shelter for the returning people. At the same time, farming cattle and tools will be purchased and loaned to the farmers to enable them to engage in production. Then, the people's armed forces will be expanded to increase their self-defense capabilities. This approach will be implemented in both the Henan-Hubei-Anhui border area and the Hunan-Hubei border area. (12th)

Shandong Provincial Library Acquires Three Rare Treasures 74

To Endure Like the Ming Lake in Fushan

Jinan Communication: Wang Xiantang, the Director of the Shandong Provincial Library, has extensive knowledge and keen discernment of bronze and stone antiquities. In recent years, he has collected rare books and antiquities, and his collection is rich and extensive. Recently, he has acquired several more kinds, which are especially rare treasures. They are recorded as follows:

Han Dynasty Cai Yong's One-Character Stone Classics 75

There are many Han Dynasty steles on the market, but very few have signatures. Only the One-Character Stone Classics, written by Cai Yong, is clearly proven. The Book of the Later Han states: [At that time, those who came to Luoyang Imperial Academy to copy it filled thousands of vehicles every day]. It can be seen how precious it was. Later, due to the long years and changes in the landscape, the stone carvings were buried underground, and very few were unearthed. In the early Qing Dynasty, Huang Xiaocun obtained a rubbing, which was the Three-Character Stone Classics from the Cao Wei Dynasty, and treasured it like a precious jade. Since the Republic of China, a certain Ding from Huang County obtained a piece of the Three-Character Stone Classics, which he also kept secretly and did not show to others. However, the One-Character Stone Classics written by Cai Yong has never been found. In 1917, the One-Character Stone Classics was unearthed. The Peking Library and Peking University each obtained a piece, with an area of ​​only one square foot, but the price was three or four thousand taels of gold. Later, Yu Youren obtained a piece for 4,300 taels of gold. A gentleman from Jiangxi was given a piece as a gift, which cost 5,000 taels of gold. These were the larger pieces. In recent years, more and more have been excavated. Ma Heng and Xu Jun, collectors in Peiping, each obtained dozens of pieces. Every complete character costs 10 gold pieces, and incomplete characters cost 7 or 8 gold pieces. Even then, people still compete to buy them. In the past two years, there has been a ban on the export of antiquities. Dozens of pieces unearthed in Luoyang are piled up and cannot be sold. A month ago, Wang Xiantang and Liu Shouzhong, a member of the Central Supervisory Committee, traveled to Luoyang and bought all the stone carvings for only 2,000 gold pieces. At that time, Zhang Puquan, a member of the Central Supervisory Committee in Luoyang, strongly advocated that Wang buy and preserve them. In the name of the Supervisory Yuan, he transported them to Shandong to be preserved by the Medical Library, which can add luster to the Ming Lake and Fushan.

Guan Zi Tang Dynasty Manuscript 76

Most of the Guan Zi books handed down in the world are 19-volume editions. The earliest 16-volume edition, according to historical records, was only seen by Han Yu. After that, it disappeared without a trace. Recently, the library purchased the Guan Zi, Erya, and other books in the Tang Dynasty manuscript from the Dunhuang Stone Chamber. The Guan Zi is especially precious. It was written by the magistrate of Dunhuang at that time and is exactly the 16-volume edition. Compared with the various editions handed down, there are many errors. The old Song and Yuan editions are not worth mentioning. The original is a handscroll, complete and undamaged, and the ink is still new. It can be called the only extant copy in the country and a rare and precious book.

Classic Expositions from the Haiyuan Pavilion 77

The Haiyuan Pavilion library of the Yang family in Liaocheng was repeatedly destroyed by wars, and there are not many books left. Among the manuscripts in its collection, there is the Classic Expositions, which is also the only extant copy in the country. In 1928, it was looted by bandits who did not cherish it and sold it cheaply to bookstores in Tianjin. Recently, it was also purchased by the library. At the same time, there are still four kinds of books that are said to be treasures from the Haiyuan Pavilion. (12th)

Suzhou 78

Tax on Brokerage Firms Harassing Merchants; Telegram Sent Requesting a Halt

The Suzhou County Associations of more than forty industries, including the brokers of southern goods, miscellaneous goods, grains, etc., because the Finance Department has changed the regulations on the tax on brokerage firms, requiring them to obtain a license for each type of goods. Strange Murder Case in a Nunnery 79

The Guandi Temple at No. 3, Sujia Village, Yongning Bridge, outside Loumen, is a nunnery. At 3:00 p.m. on the 12th, a worshiper came, claiming to be fulfilling a vow. After entering the nunnery, he took out a dollar and ordered the old nun Yan Liang's apprentice, Guigen, to go out and buy cigarettes. When Guigen returned with the cigarettes, the worshiper was standing in front of the hall, but Yan Liang was nowhere to be found. A moment later, the worshiper left. Later, Yan Liang's body was found in the well in the back, upside down. Guigen then went into the room to check and found that more than 2,000 dollars were missing. Guigen immediately reported to the police station to track down the worshiper, but he had disappeared. The police station questioned Guigen about the worshiper's background, but his statement was vague. Therefore, it is widely rumored that Guigen is suspected of being an accomplice. Guigen was sent to the branch bureau and then to the Public Security Bureau for interrogation. The District Procuratorate sent Prosecutor Shen to inspect the scene at 11:00 a.m. yesterday (13th) and examined the body of the old nun Yan Liang. It was confirmed that she had drowned after falling into the well and that there were no injuries on her body. The local authorities were ordered to collect and bury the body.

The General Labor Union of Shanghai Calls for Serious Negotiations Regarding France's Occupation of Nine Islands 90

These islands are crucial to national defense and transportation.

Negotiations should be conducted to protect inherent territory.

The Shanghai General Labor Union, in response to the French government's blatant occupation of the nine islands in southern Guangdong, which infringes upon our territory and endangers our national defense, telegraphed the central government yesterday, requesting serious negotiations. The original telegram read: "To the Executive Committee of the Central Party Headquarters of the Kuomintang, the National Government, and the Ministry of Foreign Affairs: It is reported that on the 25th of last month, the French government blatantly occupied nine small islands in southern Guangdong. This news has been received with deep indignation. It has been verified by the Guangdong provincial government that these nine islands are located south of Qiongya and are indeed our territory. They are situated between the Philippines and Annam, rich in aquatic products, and have long been inhabited by our people. Their importance to transportation and national defense is especially significant. Now, the French government is taking advantage of our nation's time of tribulation, imitating the September 18th Incident by the Japanese, and openly occupying them. This is outrageous. Moreover, the Japanese Ministry of Foreign Affairs is now collecting false evidence, hoping to get involved. If we remain silent and do not protest, then we will see imperialists gaining an inch and wanting a mile, devouring us like whales and silkworms without end. Our great territory may all be lost, leaving endless troubles for the future. Therefore, we urgently telegraph this matter, humbly requesting that you promptly conduct serious negotiations with the French government to prevent further covetousness and protect our territory. We earnestly await your response. The Shanghai General Labor Union, respectfully. First Month."

The China Merchants Steam Navigation Company's Loan Agreement with British Boxer Indemnity Signed in Nanjing 91

Transferred to Liu Hongsheng for signature.

The China Merchants Steam Navigation Company borrowed 360,000 pounds from the British Boxer Indemnity to be used for shipbuilding, with its shipbuilding assets and future income as collateral, at an annual interest rate of 5%. Interest payments will begin two years after the loan, and principal and interest will be repaid in installments thereafter, with full repayment by 1950. The agreement has already been signed by Mr. Masier, Deputy Chairman of the British Boxer Indemnity Committee, and was sent to the Ministry on the 10th for transfer to the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company, where it will be signed by the company's General Manager, Liu Hongsheng. However, after signing, it must still be forwarded to the Ministry of Finance for signature before it becomes officially effective.

According to the Ministry of Communications, the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company's business has improved since it was nationalized. General Manager Liu Hongsheng reported that the total revenue from December 21st to the end of May 22nd was over 3,364,000 yuan, an increase of over 292,000 yuan compared to the average total revenue for the same period in the previous four years. Adding the 112,500 yuan in outstanding old debts, the total increase is over 404,780 yuan. It is expected that this year's income and expenses will offset each other, and there will not be the deficits of previous years.

The Anti-Japanese Volunteers in Rehe Are Active 93

Li Haifeng's Troops Report on the Battle Situation

Popular Morale is High and the Japanese Army Suffers Great Losses

The Xinsheng News Agency reports that the Northeastern Anti-Japanese Volunteer Army has recently become active again, with frequent skirmishes with the enemy. According to a recent telegram from Li Haifeng's troops in Rehe, the situation is as follows: "On July 20th, our troops stationed at Yanghe received a report from Zhou Zixiang, Brigade Commander of Fuxin, proposing a joint attack on Lingyuan. After receiving the report, Rong Xiangchao immediately led Zhang's brigade and Yao's brigade, marching east overnight. They arrived at Guandianzi in Lingyuan early on the 24th and immediately received a report that Liang's brigade of the Southern Rehe Volunteer Army and local militias, numbering about 3,000, were engaged in fierce fighting with the Japanese army in Daerdeng. Deputy Commander Rong immediately led his troops to intercept them and mobilized local militias to encircle the Japanese. The Japanese army sent 11 planes to drop bombs, destroying 12 villages, including Chapeng, Daerdeng, and Nianfang. More than 700 residents were killed or injured, and women and children who could not escape were burned to death, a truly tragic scene. The fighting continued until the evening of the 25th. Our troops and militias, due to the overwhelming firepower of the Japanese army, broke through the encirclement at midnight and attacked the Japanese rear. At this time, Zhang Xianglin, head of the Jianping Militia, also led his troops to assist in the battle, completely surrounding the Japanese army. A bayonet charge lasted for three hours. More than 300 Japanese soldiers were killed, and the Jing'an Guerrilla Unit led by Kojima Nakano was completely annihilated. Our troops suffered relatively few casualties, while the militia suffered about 700 deaths. Members of the local Red Spear Society, even those from over 200 li away, rushed to help in the battle. The strength of popular morale is evident. Although the local losses are devastating, anti-Japanese battles have broken out throughout Rehe province. In Suidong, more than a thousand civilians massacred over 30 Japanese police and military personnel overnight. Civilians rose up on the west bank of the Lao Ha River (Chifeng Weichang). Rehe is gradually becoming tense."

Observations on the International Situation 95

The Far Eastern question will change after three years.

The Chinese people must actively build during this period.

Recently, an expert familiar with diplomacy shared his observations on the international situation, which are of great value for record-keeping, as follows: He stated that the Far Eastern question will undergo significant changes in three years. Since the September 18th Incident, Japan has dared to act recklessly and disregard everything because it seeks to realize its dream of becoming the hegemon of East Asia. At the same time, its actions have been so aggressive because it believes that its imagined enemies on land and sea (i.e., the United States and the Soviet Union) have no real ability to intervene during this period. The fact that the United States and the Soviet Union have not acted as Japan expected is supported by evidence. The London Naval Treaty stipulates a ratio of 5:5:3 (i.e., 5 for England, 5 for the United States, and 3 for Japan) in naval holdings. To this day, the United States actually does not have 50% of its allotted holdings, while Japan has exceeded its allotment. At the time, the American authorities believed they had no disputes with others and did not pay much attention. It was not until the Far Eastern question arose that they realized the inadequacy of their naval power. Since the London Treaty will expire in 1936, they are now rushing to catch up, deciding to build 32 battleships with 300 million US dollars and repair existing destroyers with 70 million, with a three-year deadline, scheduled to be completed by the end of 1936. Before the completion of the three-year naval plan, the United States will definitely not make effective interventions on the Far Eastern question. This can be asserted. At the same time, relations between England and Japan have deteriorated recently due to trade disputes, which may lead to the anticipation of England and the United States joining hands in the future. Observing this, if something happens to the Far Eastern question, Japan's navy, although strong, will likely not prevail with a ratio of 3 to 10. On the Soviet side, from 1917 to 1927, the revolutionary government's policies were disliked by various countries. However, since 1928, it has changed its policy and started the first Five-Year Plan, focusing on the construction of the Soviet Union. After the September 18th Incident, the Five-Year Plan was nearing completion, and the second Five-Year Plan was about to begin, so it was unable to intervene in the Manchurian question. Now, the relationship between various countries and the Soviet Union is gradually recovering, and the second Five-Year Plan will also be completed in 1937. By then, with internal strength and restored diplomacy, the alliance between the United States and Russia to jointly restrain Japan is also a matter of course. However, the United States and Russia do not intervene in the Far Eastern question out of love for us. Instead, it is to maintain China's market and to maintain their rights in northern Manchuria. Therefore, our country's survival depends on the next three years. We must quickly build our nation within this short period, strengthening our politics, economy, and national defense, at least to the point of being able to defend ourselves. Otherwise, if Japan is defeated, but the United States and Russia still cannot maintain their rights and objectives, they will believe that China is incapable of self-government and will build it for us, which means control. If Japan wins, it will become even more arrogant and swallow China. Therefore, the Chinese people must actively build our nation and strengthen our self-defense capabilities before the Far Eastern storm breaks out.

Qian Industry Indicates Convenience After the Abolition of the Tael and Implementation of the Yuan 96

The inflation of silver ingots is a temporary phenomenon.

According to sources in the Qian industry, since the abolition of the tael and the implementation of the yuan, the Qian industry can save one step in the process of converting taels to yuan in remittances and other transactions, which is quite convenient. However, at the beginning of implementation, silver ingots (i.e., yuanbao) are no longer circulated in the market, and they must be exchanged for new currency at the rate of 7.15 from the Central, China, and Communications Banks. However, the minting of new currency is only 100,000 yuan per day, while Shanghai has 20 million taels of silver ingots. Therefore, the exchange is very insufficient. Moreover, banks and firms from other places also use old silver ingots to settle accounts in Shanghai. Shanghai firms feel that there is a surplus of silver ingots and have no choice but to accept them, which makes them feel that there are too many yuanbao. Although a telegram has been sent to the Ministry of Finance requesting that the Central Mint increase the amount of minting, there has been no reply yet. Even if the amount is increased, it may be difficult to drastically increase it. Currently, transactions between firms are temporarily using factory bars (i.e., silver bars from the Central Mint, each bar worth 1,000 yuan) for mutual use, supplemented by the circulation of paper money. Therefore, although silver ingots are inflated, there is no feeling of illiquidity.

The Maigen Road Station Dispute Resurfaces 97

The Railway Bureau announces that the old foremen will not be reappointed.

Workers issue a declaration refusing to register.

The Shanghai-Nanjing and Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railway Administration previously caused a dispute over the cancellation of the Maigen Road Freight Station Stevedores Cooperative. After the Ministry of Railways, together with the Central Mass Movement Committee, repeatedly sent representatives Guo Zhongxing and Li Renzhu to Shanghai for investigation, the Ministry of Railways and the Mass Movement Committee mutually agreed to allow the establishment of a Maigen Road Freight Station Stevedores Office. This dispute was temporarily resolved. Yesterday, the bureau sent personnel to the station to register the workers in accordance with ministry orders. All the workers rose up in opposition, and the situation was quite serious. As a result, the dispute that had just been resolved resurfaced. The details are recorded below:

Railway Bureau Proclamation 98

The Railway Administration proclaims: For the matter of proclamation, the provisional rules for the Maigen Road Freight Station Stevedores Office have been promulgated. Now, in accordance with Article 2 of the rules, worker registration will be carried out. The registration method has been reviewed and approved by the members of the Mass Movement Guidance Committee of the Central Party Headquarters and the members of the Ministry of Railways and is hereby announced below. All stevedores at Maigen Road Freight Station must comply with this proclamation. Details of the approved worker registration method: (1) Date: August 13th to 15th; (2) Time: 8:00 a.m. to 5:00 p.m. daily; (3) Location: Maigen Road Station; (4) Procedures: Each worker must bring the original brass tag issued by the bureau and arrive at the registration office at Maigen Road Station on time. After verification, they will register in the prescribed order.

Registration Order 99

(1) Any worker who wishes to register must first go to the verification department to verify the original brass tag issued by the bureau. The verification department will then ask the worker for their name, age, native place, and family status, filling in the appropriate columns of the stevedore register. At the same time, a registration request form will be issued to the worker. (2) After receiving the registration request form, the worker must take the form to the registration department to request a number. The registration department will assign a number in order, fill it in on the registration request form, and then return the form to the worker. (3) The worker will take the numbered registration request form to the certification department, hand in the registration request form along with the brass tag, and exchange them for a registration certificate. In the future, they will use the registration certificate to exchange for a new brass tag and work permit. (4) The worker will take the registration certificate to the photo department to request a photo.

Department Procedures 100

(1) Verification Department: After verifying that the brass tag held by the worker requesting registration matches the individual, a registration request form will be issued and given to the worker to take to the registration department. (2) Registration Department: Upon receiving the worker's registration request form and verifying that it is correct, it shall inquire about the worker's resume and family status, fill in the appropriate columns of the stevedore register, and then assign a number in order. The assigned number shall be entered in the worker register and registration request form. The numbered registration request form shall then be returned.

The import of Japanese goods to the Yangtze River reaches in July surged two-fold 101

Total volume reaches 12,622 tons

Xinsheng News Agency reports that in the recent two months, the import of Japanese goods into Shanghai has surged. According to accurate surveys by the Japanese, the imports in July were the highest this year. Last month, the Japanese shipping company Nippon Yusen's imported cargo totaled 18 ships in regular service, carrying a total of 12,622 tons of Japanese goods to Shanghai. This is an increase of 280 tons compared to the 11,383 tons imported in June. Among these goods, 2,328 tons were transshipped to various ports along the Yangtze River, more than twice the 510 tons imported to the Yangtze ports in June. Recently, the Japanese officials and merchants have felt that this increase in imports is a sign of improvement in Sino-Japanese relations and are mostly optimistic because it clearly demonstrates the decline of the anti-Japanese movement among the Chinese people. Regarding the categories of increased imports, sugar increased threefold compared to June. Cotton cloth and various textiles totaled 1,246 bales, which is a slight decrease compared to the previous month. Paper products totaled 1,387 pieces, an increase of over 200 pieces compared to June. Cotton totaled 850 bales (over 50 of which were Egyptian cotton, the rest being American cotton). Domestic Japanese cotton yarn merchants are currently rejecting Indian cotton, so the small number is due to other reasons. However, the most significant increase was in the import of chemical raw materials, specifically acids. In June, the total was less than 2,000 boxes, but in July it increased to 8,275 boxes. This reflects the improvement of the match industry and the cotton textile industry. Other goods, such as seafood, totaled 3,770 boxes, with high-priced shark fins increasing due to the reduction of import taxes. However, the Japanese observation on the increased imports is that the internal unrest in the Yangtze River interior and the decline of the rural economy prevent even larger imports.

To the worker. (3) Certification Department: Based on the registration request form, after numbering it, the certification shall give a registration certificate to the worker. (4) Photo Department: Take a photo of the worker based on the registration certificate.

Work Assignment 102

(1) Prepare the registration book, to be handled by Deputy Director Xie of the Traffic Department. Worker Declaration 103

All the workers at Maigen Road issued a declaration yesterday regarding the resolution formulated by the Central Mass Movement Guidance Committee and the Ministry of Railways and the deprivation of the right to be elected of the chief foreman Shen Yuqing and others. The declaration said: "Since the Maigen Road Station stevedores abolished the contract system and organized a cooperative five years ago, the chief foreman Shen Yuqing and others have led all the workers to abide by the railway regulations. The reason why all the workers can follow them is that the four chief foremen are fair and never favor anyone. The four chief foremen's external actions are absolutely based on the wishes of all the workers, which is especially trusted and supported by all our workers. After the Railway Bureau restored the contract system, the public was indignant, and finally, relying on the four chief foremen's efforts to persuade them, they continued to work as usual and, according to the guidance of the higher-level Party Department and trade union, argued with reason and waited quietly for a solution. Now, the Central Committee and the Ministry of Railways have formulated four solutions: (1) The contractors sent by the Railway Bureau must be cancelled; (2) The old cooperative should be changed into an office; (3) The office should elect two chief foremen to preside over everything; (4) The original four foremen shall not be elected as foremen after the reorganization. The fourth point, that the original four foremen shall not be elected as foremen after the reorganization, is what all our workers vow to oppose to the death. The chief foreman Shen Yuqing and others have traveled around for the contractor Yang Hengzhen. It is their duty to safeguard the interests of the workers. Unexpectedly, they have been envied, as if they could not be happy unless the four of them were removed, as if the four of them were Yang Hengzhen's funeral objects, and the deprivation of the right to be elected is without any basis. During this period of political tutelage, this kind of unfeeling and unreasonable method cannot exist. This is what all our workers will never accept. Now, the chief foreman Shen Yuqing and others have expressed their abandonment of the right to elect in order to clarify their intentions. It is important to know that it is not easy to say leave or stay when entrusted by all the workers. Therefore, we still order them to continue to be responsible and not be tempted or threatened. All seven hundred workers vow to be their backing."

Refusal to Register 104

Immediately, eight registration tables were set up in the freight station, and the police chief Ma of the Railway Police Department led the railway police to maintain order. The factory has voluntarily sent them for safekeeping

"There are eight tons in the iron bucket. Without the consent of the association, we will never use it privately and will obey your instructions. There was also a pledge that we will never buy enemy goods and will accept the most severe punishment from the association if we import them privately. All of them were stamped with the factory's seal.

Reconstruction of the North Station on Two Railways Completed 112

Painting Started Yesterday, Inauguration Ceremony Scheduled

Traffic Department Decides to Move in for Office Work Before the End of the Month

The Beijing-Shanghai and Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railway Administration, with the approval of the Ministry, reconstructed the Shanghai North Station. The project has been completed, painting has begun, and an inauguration ceremony has been scheduled. The Traffic Department has decided to move in for office work before the end of the month. Details are recorded below.

Project Completed 113

The reconstruction of the Shanghai North Station on the two railways was contracted by the China-South Construction Company. It was the old site destroyed by the Japanese army during the Shanghai battle, measuring 200 feet long and 80 feet deep, with a hall 21 feet high, 60 feet long, and 80 feet deep. The offices on both sides are 10 feet high, and the upper floor is 11 feet high. As of yesterday, the project has been completed and painting has begun. It is expected that all painting and other work will be fully completed before the 25th of this month and handed over to the Two Railways Bureau for acceptance.

Moving in for Office Work 114

The Two Railways Traffic Department temporarily converted the tin houses opposite the North Station into offices after the North Station was destroyed. Now that the reconstruction of the North Station has been completed, it has been decided to move in for office work before the end of this month. The layout plan has been decided. The north end of the hall will be the offices of the director and deputy director of the Traffic Department, and the south end will be the office of the business section of the Traffic Department. The offices of the Traffic Department and various sections will be on the second floor. As for the ticket office and luggage room, they will remain in their original locations. The inauguration ceremony is scheduled for September 1st, and all circles are invited to visit.

Soliciting Names of Initiators from All Circles

The Zhuanqiao Farmers' Education Center in the Third Public Education District of Shanghai County believes that native cloth is woven by village women, is cheap and durable, and is the most economical clothing material. Impersonating Court Investigators and Extorting Lawsuit Plaintiffs 116

Recently, Such Incidents Have Been Repeatedly Heard

Huang Fan Recently Deceived

The Court Will Strictly Investigate

Recently, there have often been unscrupulous people impersonating investigators from the First Special District Court to intimidate and extort money from ordinary lawsuit plaintiffs. Many victims are unwilling to investigate further even after realizing they have been deceived because the losses are not significant, which makes these people bolder. According to various sources, the method of fraud is roughly the same. Before implementing the fraud, they enter the court hearing the case, sit high in the press gallery, hold a pencil, and act like they are taking notes. Government officials from the judge down think they are news reporters, and unless the case is prohibited from being heard, they are naturally not convenient to interfere. Thus, the swindler can fully know the contents of the case, choose the cautious party involved, and silently recognize them. The next morning, they read various newspapers. If they see a report of the case they are paying attention to, they follow the address of the plaintiff in the report and visit them. If they are met by the person they saw in court, they immediately state the details of the case and then claim that they are investigators sent by the court and are specifically investigating various points in the case. The person sees that their words mostly match the lawsuit and deeply believes that they are indeed investigators, and they treat them very kindly. They feel that their plan has been sold, and they further demand investigation fees or transportation fees, which amount to between five and six yuan. People suspect fraud even less because the amount is small. Even if they encounter one or two shrewd people who question why they are not wearing a uniform or ask for a receipt, the swindler responds at any time and makes excuses. Such fraud has been repeatedly heard recently. A few days ago, Fan, the wife of Huang Yichu, a Guangdong native, and Wu Lansheng, a neighbor, were involved in a lawsuit due to a dispute and also encountered this fraud, losing over seven silver dollars. When Liu Yugui of the First Special Court continued the hearing of the case yesterday, Huang Fan stated in court that she had been defrauded, just like the aforementioned situation. She said that the person was wearing a suit and claimed to be named Yuan, coming to summon my son Huang Keming to the case. I told him that my son had gone to Guangdong. Before leaving, the person demanded an investigation fee of five yuan, seven jiao, and five fen, and two yuan for transportation, and said that he needed to go to the opposing party for investigation and also collect the same fees from the opposing party. When I asked for a receipt, the person said that you women are ignorant and it is not convenient to give a receipt. Judge Liu then asked Wu Lansheng whether such a person had come before. Wu shook his head frequently. Judge Liu was furious that someone dared to borrow the court's name to deceive and swindle, and immediately announced the court's handling procedures, saying that the court must give a formal receipt for any fees collected, and court staff must wear uniforms when going out to work. If either of these two items is missing, it is an impersonation. The court has repeatedly issued orders regarding such incidents. Lawsuit plaintiffs should immediately hand over those who encounter such deception to the police station for legal handling and must not show any leniency. He also instructed that the case be adjourned and thoroughly investigated. It is heard that the court will strictly crack down on listeners in the future, except for those who have long-term listening tickets.

Gentlemen of Beiqiao 117

Please Preserve Tang Dynasty Monuments

Beiqiao Bell Tower Said to Be a Tang Dynasty Building

One Generation's Historical Site Presented to County Government for Repair

The Beiqiao Township Bell Tower in Shanghai was built in the Tang Dynasty and is recorded in the county annals. However, it has been in disrepair for a long time and is increasingly collapsing. Previously, the Beiqiao Township Office and local people presented a request to the Shanghai County Government to allocate funds for repairs in order to preserve the monuments, but the County Government was limited by funds and had no funds to allocate, which has been delayed until now without starting repairs. The collapse of the bell tower is also increasing day by day. Now that the County Government has moved to the new Shanghai area in Beiqiao, it is appropriately facing the bell tower, but there is a distinction between the new and the collapsed, which has attracted the attention of local gentlemen. A few days ago, local people in Beiqiao specifically presented another request to the County Government, urging it to immediately allocate funds to start repairs, in order to preserve the monuments and restore the old appearance, so that the historical sites of one generation can be passed down permanently.

Wu asked if any such people had come before, Wu shook his head frequently, and Judge Liu was furious that someone dared to borrow the court's name to deceive and swindle, and immediately announced the court's handling procedures, saying that the court must give a formal receipt for any fees collected, and court staff must wear uniforms when going out to work. If either of these two items is missing, it is an impersonation. The court has repeatedly issued orders regarding such incidents. Lawsuit plaintiffs should immediately hand over those who encounter such deception to the police station for legal handling and must not show any leniency. He also instructed that the case be adjourned and thoroughly investigated. It is heard that the court will strictly crack down on listeners in the future, except for those who have long-term listening tickets.

It is found that Article 7 of the Shanghai Housing Leasing Rules promulgated by Your Office states: [All small rent digging fees are strictly prohibited.] Article 10: [If the landlord demolishes and builds a house, he should apply to the Bureau of Public Works for approval and notify each tenant to move out three months in advance, and the last two months' rent should be waived, but this is not limited to special agreements longer than the provisions of this article.] Article 11: [When the sublessor receives the notice from the landlord in accordance with Article 10, he shall immediately notify the subtenant and shall waive the rent in accordance with Article 10.] Article 12: [Except as provided in Article 10, the landlord or sublessor shall not force a tenant or subtenant who pays rent to move out. A Flower Gambling Scheme 135

As a result, he was arrested.

The flower gambling, which is more harmful than floods and fierce beasts, has been popular again recently. Even the villages and towns near this port have established listening tubes and boats. Therefore, gamblers who are deeply addicted to flower gambling hope to obtain huge profits, and they are all busy playing the tide. (The word "playing the tide" refers to asking the gods, divination, praying for dreams, drawing lots, and various despicable acts.) They are like crazy people, almost forgetting to eat and sleep. Liu Lushi, a woman living at No. 47, Chunyangli, Zhoujiaqiao, West Shanghai, has also been deeply addicted to flower gambling recently. She has made a desperate bet, and she has lost a lot. Therefore, her efforts to play the tide, such as asking the gods and divination, have not been successful. A few days ago, she suddenly learned that Li Amao, a young man living at No. 39 in the same neighborhood, could carry a tube (carrying a tube means that a god is possessed and predicts the name of the flower). It has been repeatedly tested and is known to the people nearby. Therefore, the clan was very happy when she heard about it, thinking that she could make a huge profit through this. So, at about 3:00 AM the day before yesterday, she invited Li to her home, burned incense and kowtowed. Li immediately babbled, as if a god was possessed. Then, he said that the flower gambling could hit the two doors of "Ban Gui" and "Feng Chun". The clan kowtowed in thanks, and because she threw a lot of numbers, she ordered her husband, Liu Ada, to take the money to Shanghai and hit it in the big tube. Unexpectedly, in the evening, she received a fast horse report that it was indeed the above-mentioned two doors. So, Liu won 600 yuan for "Ban Gui" and 1,000 yuan for "Feng Chun", which was spread far and wide. Until the next morning (the day before yesterday morning), Li thought that the Liu clan had already obtained a huge amount of money, why there was still no reward sent. Li went to the clan and said, "Since yesterday until now, the god is still possessed and has not retreated, and the body feels quite uncomfortable. I need to ask a doctor to treat it." Because her husband had not returned to Shanghai and she did not know how much she had won, she refused with harsh words. Not only did she not reward or treat him, but she also drove him away. When Li's mother, Zhu, heard about it, she immediately rushed over and twisted Liu Chenshi to the police and detained her in the sixth district, accusing Liu Chenshi of forcing her son Li Amao to ask the gods for flowers, causing harm to his body. After District Officer Jiang interrogated her, he immediately prepared a document and sent it to the General Bureau for interrogation because the case involved flower gambling.
